prePlayerSetup(blocking){if(blocking&&adContext.get(\\\'opts.wadHMD\\\')){hmdRecLoader.setOnReady(function(){setupPlayer();});return;}if(!blocking&&bidders&&bidders.isEnabled()){bidders.runOnBiddingReady(function(){bidParams=bidders.updateSlotTargeting(featuredVideoSlotName);setupPlayer();});return;}setupPlayer();}trackingOptIn.pushToUserConsentQueue(function(){if(adsApi){adsApi.waitForAdStackResolve().then(setupPlayer);return;}if(!adContext||!adContext.get(\\\'opts.showAds\\\')){setupPlayer();return;}if(!hmdRecLoader||!adContext.get(\\\'opts.babDetectionDesktop\\\')){\\nprePlayerSetup(false);}else{doc.addEventListener(\\\'bab.blocking\\\',function(){prePlayerSetup(true);});doc.addEventListener(\\\'bab.not_blocking\\\',function(){prePlayerSetup(false);});}});});</script>\\n\\t\\t</div>\\n\\t\\t\\t</div>\\n</div>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t<div <small>(child)</small></div>\\n</div>\\n</aside>\\n\\n<div class="quote">\\n<dl><dd><span title="Source:You Win or You Die">"<i>When you play the game of thrones, you win or you die. There is no middle ground.</i>"</span>\\n</dd><dd>&#8213;Cersei Lannister to <a href="/wiki/Eddard_Stark" title="Eddard Stark">Eddard Stark</a><span class="noprint"><sup><a href="/wiki/You_Win_or_You_Die" title="You Win or You Die">[src]</a></sup></span></div>\\n</dd></dl>\\n<p>Queen <b>Cersei I Lannister</b> is the widow of <a href="/wiki/King_of_the_Andals,_the_Rhoynar,_and_the_First_Men" title="King of the Andals, the Rhoynar, and the First Men">King</a> <a href="/wiki/Robert_Baratheon" title="Robert Baratheon">Robert Baratheon</a>, with whom she had <a href="/wiki/Baratheon_(son_of_Robert)" title="Baratheon (son of Robert)">her sole trueborn child</a>, and Queen of the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Kingdoms" title="Seven Kingdoms">Seven Kingdoms</a>. She is the daughter of Lord <a href="/wiki/Tywin_Lannister" title="Tywin Lannister">Tywin Lannister</a>, twin sister of <a href="/wiki/Jaime_Lannister" title="Jaime Lannister">Jaime Lannister</a> and elder sister of <a href="/wiki/Tyrion_Lannister" title="Tyrion Lannister">Tyrion Lannister</a>. She had an <a href="/wiki/Incest" title="Incest">incestuous</a> relationship with Jaime, who is secretly the father of her three <a href="/wiki/Bastard" title="Bastard" class="mw-redirect">bastard</a> children, <a href="/wiki/Joffrey_Baratheon" title="Joffrey Baratheon">Joffrey</a>, <a href="/wiki/Myrcella_Baratheon" title="Myrcella Baratheon">Myrcella</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tommen_Baratheon" title="Tommen Baratheon">Tommen</a>.\\n</p><p>After the <a href="/wiki/Poison" title="Poison">poisoning</a> of her <a href="/wiki/Purple_Wedding" title="Purple Wedding">elder</a> <a href="/wiki/Assassination_of_Myrcella_Baratheon" title="Assassination of Myrcella Baratheon">children</a> in the later stages of the <a href="/wiki/War_of_the_Five_Kings" title="War of the Five Kings">War of the Five Kings</a> and Tommen\\\'s suicide in the wake of the <a href="/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Great_Sept_of_Baelor" title="Destruction of the Great Sept of Baelor">destruction of the Great Sept of Baelor</a>, Cersei assumed the throne under the name of <b>Cersei of the House Lannister, the First of Her Name, Queen of the Andals and the First Men, Protector of the Seven Kingdoms</b>, making her the twentieth ruler of the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Kingdoms" title="Seven Kingdoms">Seven Kingdoms</a> (as well as the first officially recognized Queen Regnant in the history of <a href="/wiki/Westeros" title="Westeros">Westeros</a>). \\n</p>\\n<nav id="toc" class="toc" data-loaded="false"><div id="toctitle"><h2>Contents</h2><span class="toctoggle">[<a href="#" class="internal" id="togglelink" data-show="show" data-hide="hide">show</a>]</span></div><ol></ol></nav>\\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Biography">Biography</span></h2>\\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Background">Background</span></h3>\\n<p>Cersei is the only daughter and eldest child of Lord Tywin Lannister and his wife <a href="/wiki/Joanna_Lannister" title="Joanna Lannister">Joanna Lannister</a>, who was also his cousin. Tywin is the head of <a href="/wiki/House_Lannister" title="House Lannister">House Lannister</a>, the richest man in the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Kingdoms" title="Seven Kingdoms">Seven Kingdoms</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lord_Paramount_of_the_Westerlands" title="Lord Paramount of the Westerlands">Lord Paramount of the Westerlands</a>. <a href="/wiki/The_Westerlands" title="The Westerlands">The Westerlands</a> are one of the constituent regions of the Seven Kingdoms and House Lannister is one of the <a href="/wiki/Great_Houses" title="Great Houses" class="mw-redirect">Great Houses</a> of the realm. Cersei is the elder twin of <a href="/wiki/Jaime_Lannister" title="Jaime Lannister">Ser Jaime Lannister</a> and the elder sister of <a href="/wiki/Tyrion_Lannister" title="Tyrion Lannister">Tyrion Lannister</a>. She was raised in privilege in the family seat of <a href="/wiki/Casterly_Rock" title="Casterly Rock">Casterly Rock</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Cersei_viewers_guide_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cersei_viewers_guide-1">[2]</a></sup> She is known for her great beauty.\\n</p><p>Cersei\\\'s mother died when she was four years old, after giving birth to her younger brother Tyrion. Like her father, Cersei has always blamed Tyrion for her mother\\\'s death and deeply resents that her mother died so that Tyrion would be brought into the world.<sup id="cite_ref-The_Night_Lands_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-The_Night_Lands-2">[3]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Tyrion_viewers_guide_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tyrion_viewers_guide-3">[4]</a></sup> As for Cersei\\\'s father Tywin, he was constantly away from home during her childhood and teenage years, serving as <a href="/wiki/Hand_of_the_King" title="Hand of the King">Hand of the King</a> at the capital, with only infrequent visits back to his seat at Casterly Rock. Coupled with the death of her mother, this meant that Cersei and her two brothers were primarily raised by servants attached to House Lannister. She began an incestuous relationship with Jaime in her youth which has continued despite her marriage.<sup id="cite_ref-Cersei_viewers_guide_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cersei_viewers_guide-1">[2]</a></sup> While Cersei has had other partners, Jaime has always kept himself strictly for her.<sup id="cite_ref-E17_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E17-4">[5]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/7a/YoungCersei%26Melara.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150413035220" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="YoungCersei&amp;amp;Melara"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="YoungCersei%26Melara.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="YoungCersei&amp;amp;Melara.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/7a/YoungCersei%26Melara.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150413035220"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/7a/YoungCersei%26Melara.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150413035220" \\t alt="YoungCersei&amp;amp;Melara"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="YoungCersei%26Melara.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="YoungCersei&amp;amp;Melara.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:YoungCersei%26Melara.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei hoped she would marry Rhaegar Targaryen, or at least become Queen at any rate.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>When she was about fifteen, Cersei and her friend <a href="/wiki/Melara_Hetherspoon" title="Melara Hetherspoon">Melara</a> visited <a href="/wiki/Maggy" title="Maggy">Maggy</a>, a woods witch and reputed fortune teller dwelling in a hut deep in a forest close to Casterly Rock. Melara was reluctant, but Cersei convinced her to go. After rudely awakening her and insisting on having her future foretold, Maggy tasted a drop of her blood and revealed to Cersei she wouldn\\\'t marry <a href="/wiki/Rhaegar_Targaryen" title="Rhaegar Targaryen">"the Prince"</a> but <a href="/wiki/Robert_Baratheon" title="Robert Baratheon">"the King"</a>, and while the king would have twenty children, she would bear only three children who will wear golden crowns as well as golden shrouds. Finally, she revealed to Cersei that although she would indeed be Queen, she would be cast down by another, younger and more beautiful queen.<sup id="cite_ref-S5EP01_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S5EP01-5">[6]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c8/Robert_Cersei_wedding.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120603184148" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Robert Cersei wedding"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Robert_Cersei_wedding.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Robert Cersei wedding.jpg" \\t \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Robert_Cersei_wedding.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei marries Robert Baratheon.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>After the end of <a href="/wiki/Robert%27s_Rebellion" title="Robert\\\'s Rebellion">the civil war</a> which ended the reign of <a href="/wiki/House_Targaryen" title="House Targaryen">House Targaryen</a>, Cersei was married to <a href="/wiki/Robert_Baratheon" title="Robert Baratheon">King Robert Baratheon</a>, a political marriage Robert agreed to in thanks for her father\\\'s <a href="/wiki/Sack_of_King%27s_Landing" title="Sack of King\\\'s Landing">last-minute alliance</a>. She was only 19 when she married Robert and became Queen.<sup id="cite_ref-E18_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E18-6">[7]</a></sup> At first, Cersei was infatuated with the handsome Robert, but their love began to wane when he called her "<a href="/wiki/Lyanna_Stark" title="Lyanna Stark">Lyanna</a>" on their wedding night.<sup id="cite_ref-E7_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E7-7">[8]</a></sup> She nevertheless bore Robert a <a href="/wiki/Cersei%27s_black-haired_son" title="Cersei\\\'s black-haired son" class="mw-redirect">son</a> who died shortly after his birth. Cersei was devastated by the loss of her son and refused to have the body taken from her, forcing Robert to hold her while they took her son from her.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-8">[9]</a></sup> In time, Cersei\\\'s feelings for Robert turned to hatred and she returned to her brother as a result. Her three children, <a href="/wiki/Joffrey_Baratheon" title="Joffrey Baratheon">Joffrey</a>, <a href="/wiki/Myrcella_Baratheon" title="Myrcella Baratheon">Myrcella</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tommen_Baratheon" title="Tommen Baratheon">Tommen</a>, are officially Robert\\\'s, but in reality are the products of her incestuous relationship with Jaime.\\n</p>\\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Season_1"><a href="/wiki/Season_1" title="Season 1">Season 1</a></span></h3>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a comforts Cersei during Jon Arryn\\\'s funeral.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>In <a href="/wiki/King%27s_Landing" title="King\\\'s Landing">King\\\'s Landing</a>, Queen Cersei watches the <a href="/wiki/Silent_sisters" title="Silent sisters" class="mw-redirect">silent sisters</a> preparing the body of Lord <a href="/wiki/Jon_Arryn" title="Jon Arryn">Jon Arryn</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Hand_of_the_King" title="Hand of the King">Hand of the King</a>, for burial. She and her twin brother, Jaime, discuss the situation and wonder if Jon told anyone else about what he had discovered. Jaime tells her not to worry, since if the King knew the truth they\\\'d be dead already, and that Robert will simply choose a new Hand of the King everything will go on as normal. She suggests that Jaime could be the next Hand, but Jaime refuses, citing the position as too much responsibility and danger.<sup id="cite_ref-E1_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E1-9">[10]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei arrives in Winterfell.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p><a href="/wiki/King_Robert" title="King Robert" class="mw-redirect">King Robert</a> decides to travel to Winterfell and ask his best friend, Lord <a href="/wiki/Eddard_Stark" title="Eddard Stark">Eddard Stark</a>, to become the new Hand, as well as proposing that his son <a href="/wiki/Joffrey_Baratheon" title="Joffrey Baratheon">Joffrey</a> marry Eddard\\\'s eldest daughter, <a href="/wiki/Sansa_Stark" title="Sansa Stark">Sansa</a>. Cersei, Jaime, and a retinue of courtiers accompany him. When the royal party arrives at <a href="/wiki/Winterfell" title="Winterfell">Winterfell</a> (the seat of <a href="/wiki/House_Stark" title="House Stark">House Stark</a>) a month later, Eddard presents his household to Robert and Cersei, who is greeted much more formally than Robert.\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a Catelyn observe Robert\\\'s actions.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>After initial greetings, Robert demands to see the crypts and pay his respects to his former betrothed, <a href="/wiki/Lyanna_Stark" title="Lyanna Stark">Lyanna Stark</a>, stoking Cersei\\\'s impatience, eager to rest after a month\\\'s travel. After Robert and Eddard depart, Cersei sends Jaime to find their younger brother <a href="/wiki/Tyrion_Lannister" title="Tyrion Lannister">Tyrion</a>, who has become distracted at the local brothel. That evening, a great feast is held and Cersei and <a href="/wiki/Catelyn_Stark" title="Catelyn Stark">Catelyn Stark</a> exchange cordial words. Cersei seems impressed by Sansa, thinking that she will be a great success at court.\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/15/Cersei-and-Jaime-lannister.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161011122813" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Cersei-and-Jaime-lannister"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cersei-and-Jaime-lannister.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Cersei-and-Jaime-lannister.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/15/Cersei-and-Jaime-lannister.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161011122813"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/15/Cersei-and-Jaime-lannister.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161011122813" \\t alt="Cersei-and-Jaime-lannister"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cersei-and-Jaime-lannister.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Cersei-and-Jaime-lannister.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Cersei-and-Jaime-lannister.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei makes love with her Jaime.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>The next morning, Eddard and Robert go hunting, leaving the castle largely empty. Cersei and Jaime liaise in derelict tower. <a href="/wiki/Bran_Stark" title="Bran Stark">Bran Stark</a> climbs the tower and finds them engaged in sexual intercourse. He is caught watching by Cersei, and Jaime grabs him. Whilst Cersei immediately becomes worried that their secret will be exposed, Jaime feigns Bran with a sense of safety. He asks how old Bran is. When Bran replies "ten", Jaime sighs and pushes him out of the window, musing, "The things I do for love."<sup id="cite_ref-E1_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E1-9">[10]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/3f/CerseiScoldsTyrionTK.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20190406214133" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="CerseiScoldsTyrionTK"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="CerseiScoldsTyrionTK.PNG" \\tdata-image-name="CerseiScoldsTyrionTK.PNG" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/3f/CerseiScoldsTyrionTK.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190406214133"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="81"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/3f/CerseiScoldsTyrionTK.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190406214133" \\t alt="CerseiScoldsTyrionTK"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="CerseiScoldsTyrionTK.PNG" \\tdata-image-name="CerseiScoldsTyrionTK.PNG" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="81"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:CerseiScoldsTyrionTK.PNG" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei scolds Tyrion.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>A month later, at breakfast, Tyrion tells his family that Bran is expected to live and notes his sibling\\\'s guarded reactions to the news. Cersei notes that it no mercy to let the boy live, after which Tyrion snidely remarks that only the Gods know his fate. Tyrion then crudely tells his family what he plans to do whilst at <a href="/wiki/The_Wall" title="The Wall">the Wall</a>, and although Tommen and Myrcella laugh, Cersei assures them away from his "filth". In response to Tyrion\\\'s information, Cersei visits Catelyn, who is sitting vigil for Bran. Cersei tells Catelyn that <a href="/wiki/Cersei%27s_black-haired_son" title="Cersei\\\'s black-haired son" class="mw-redirect">her first child</a>, a beautiful, black-haired boy, died of a fever. \\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/2a/102_TK.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190417160004" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="102 TK"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="102_TK.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="102 TK.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/2a/102_TK.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190417160004"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="119"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/2a/102_TK.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190417160004" \\t alt="102 TK"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="102_TK.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="102 TK.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="119"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:102_TK.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei orders the execution of Lady in the place of Nymeria.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>She and Robert were grief-stricken and her prayers and tears were for naught. She offers to pray for Bran\\\'s survival, hoping that this time <a href="/wiki/Faith_of_the_Seven" title="Faith of the Seven">the gods</a> will listen. The royal party sets out for King\\\'s Landing, now joined by Eddard, Sansa and <a href="/wiki/Arya_Stark" title="Arya Stark">Arya</a>. However, an incident between Arya\\\'s <a href="/wiki/Direwolf" title="Direwolf" class="mw-redirect">direwolf</a> and Joffrey on the <a href="/wiki/Kingsroad" title="Kingsroad">Kingsroad</a> escalates into an argument between Cersei and Eddard. Robert defuses the situation by agreeing that he and Eddard will attend to their own discipline. Cersei insists that the direwolf must be killed. When <a href="/wiki/Nymeria_(direwolf)" title="Nymeria (direwolf)">Nymeria</a> cannot be found (Arya having driven her off to protect her), Cersei has Sansa\\\'s wolf, <a href="/wiki/Lady" title="Lady">Lady</a>, killed instead. A furious Eddard attends to the matter himself to spare Lady a much more grisly death at the hands of <a href="/wiki/Ilyn_Payne" title="Ilyn Payne">Ilyn Payne</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-8">[9]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/61/Cersei-joffrey.png/revision/latest?cb=20110626071454" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Cersei-joffrey"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cersei-joffrey.png" \\tdata-image-name="Cersei-joffrey.png" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/61/Cersei-joffrey.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110626071454"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="126"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/61/Cersei-joffrey.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110626071454" \\t alt="Cersei-joffrey"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cersei-joffrey.png" \\tdata-image-name="Cersei-joffrey.png" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="126"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Cersei-joffrey.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei advises Joffrey.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Arriving back at court, Cersei talks to Joffrey about the incident on the Kingsroad. She tells him that when he is king, the truth will be whatever he decides it will be. Joffrey tells her that he thinks there will be trouble with the Starks, and that when he is king he\\\'ll double their taxes, force them to contribute to a standing army and, if they should object, he\\\'d crush them. Cersei elucidates that <a href="/wiki/The_North" title="The North">the North</a> is too vast and wild to be militarily conquered by outsiders. She cautions Joffrey that he will need to be cleverer as king. She also advises him to be kind to Sansa to avoid causing trouble for later, and concludes that "anyone who isn\\\'t us is an enemy." A raven arrives in King\\\'s Landing with news of Bran\\\'s recovery. Cersei fears he will expose their secret, but Jaime comforts her.<sup id="cite_ref-E3_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E3-10">[11]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/f6/House_Baratheon_of_King%27s_Landing.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130102203425" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="House Baratheon of King&amp;#039;s Landing"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="House_Baratheon_of_King%27s_Landing.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="House Baratheon of King&#39;s Landing.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/f6/House_Baratheon_of_King%27s_Landing.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130102203425"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="101"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/f6/House_Baratheon_of_King%27s_Landing.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130102203425" \\t alt="House Baratheon of King&amp;#039;s Landing"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="House_Baratheon_of_King%27s_Landing.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="House Baratheon of King&#39;s Landing.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="101"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:House_Baratheon_of_King%27s_Landing.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei attends the tournament with her immediate family.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>At the <a href="/wiki/Tournament" title="Tournament">tournament</a>, a drunken Robert embarrasses Cersei, causing her to leave. She visits Eddard at his chambers, remarking at how the Hand is not at his own tournament. Though Cersei attempts to start the conversation in an attempt to put the incident on theKingsroadbehind them, Eddard correctly deduces that she has an ulterior motive for her visit. Cersei then wonders aloud to Eddard what his true purpose is for being at King\\\'s Landing, as she knows how little Starks enjoy being in the capital. When Eddard tells her he is there to faithfully serve their King, Cersei remarks that just as his brotherBrandonwas born to lead, Eddard was born to follow.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">[12]</a></sup>\\n</p><p>Cersei and Robert share a drink and discuss the threat from the <a href="/wiki/Dothraki" title="Dothraki">Dothraki</a> now that <a href="/wiki/Daenerys_Targaryen" title="Daenerys Targaryen">Daenerys Targaryen</a> is married and pregnant. Cersei also tells Robert that at the start of their marriage she truly loved him, even after their first boy died, for quite a while. He says he knows, but could never love her back due to his feelings for <a href="/wiki/Lyanna_Stark" title="Lyanna Stark">Lyanna Stark</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">[13]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/5e/Cersei_and_Robert.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160814015948" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Cersei and Robert"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cersei_and_Robert.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Cersei and Robert.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/5e/Cersei_and_Robert.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160814015948"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="102"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/5e/Cersei_and_Robert.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160814015948" \\t alt="Cersei and Robert"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cersei_and_Robert.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Cersei and Robert.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="102"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Cersei_and_Robert.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei and Robert visit Ned.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Cersei and King Robert visit Eddard as he recovers from wounds sustained fighting Jaime and his guards. Cersei is furious with Eddard for having her brother Tyrion arrested and for fighting with Jaime, but Eddard is unrepentant. Finding Robert unresponsive to this, she scolds him. He then hits her across the face, leaving an obvious mark. She marks that this only increases her integrity, but Robert threatens her to silence, promising to hit her again if she speaks of it. <sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">[14]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/65/Cerseiandned.png/revision/latest?cb=20110622112109" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Cerseiandned"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cerseiandned.png" \\tdata-image-name="Cerseiandned.png" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/65/Cerseiandned.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110622112109"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="127"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/65/Cerseiandned.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110622112109" \\t alt="Cerseiandned"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cerseiandned.png" \\tdata-image-name="Cerseiandned.png" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="127"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Cerseiandned.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei reveals the truth to Ned.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Eddard confronts Cersei and tells her he knows her children are fathered by Jaime. She does not deny it, instead saying that she and her brother belong together, always. Cersei says she did love Robert at first, but on their wedding night he whispered Lyanna\\\'s name, which soured their relationship afterwards. Eddard advises her to leave King\\\'s Landing before Robert returns from a hunt, as he will then tell Robert the truth. Cersei instead warns him that "In the game of thrones, you win or you die."<sup id="cite_ref-E7_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E7-7">[8]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/93/Cersei_%26_Joffrey_1x07.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110531154124" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Cersei &amp;amp; Joffrey 1x07"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cersei_%26_Joffrey_1x07.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Cersei &amp;amp; Joffrey 1x07.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/93/Cersei_%26_Joffrey_1x07.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110531154124"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="100"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/93/Cersei_%26_Joffrey_1x07.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110531154124" \\t alt="Cersei &amp;amp; Joffrey 1x07"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cersei_%26_Joffrey_1x07.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Cersei &amp;amp; Joffrey 1x07.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="100"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Cersei_%26_Joffrey_1x07.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei serves as Queen Regent following the death of Robert.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Robert is mortally wounded on the hunt. Cersei is concerned that Eddard will tell Robert the truth, but Ned chooses to spare his friend further pain. Robert names Eddard Protector of the Realm and regent. Upon Robert\\\'s death Cersei quickly installs Joffrey on the throne. Eddard tries to reveal the truth with the help of <a href="/wiki/Petyr_Baelish" title="Petyr Baelish">Petyr \\\'Littlefinger\\\' Baelish</a>, but Baelish betrays him and sides with Cersei. Eddard is arrested and imprisoned, while his guards are killed.<sup id="cite_ref-E7_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E7-7">[8]</a></sup>\\n</p><p>Cersei persuades Sansa to write a letter asking her brother <a href="/wiki/Robb_Stark" title="Robb Stark">Robb</a> to bend the knee to Joffrey in return for her father\\\'s life. Sansa agrees, but the plan backfires, as the letter merely encourages Robb to raise an army and march into the <a href="/wiki/Riverlands" title="Riverlands" class="mw-redirect">Riverlands</a> to confront the Lannister armies directly. In open court, Cersei encourages Sansa to make a new plea to Joffrey for her father\\\'s life. Joffrey agrees to spare him and let him join the <a href="/wiki/Night%27s_Watch" title="Night\\\'s Watch">Night\\\'s Watch</a>, if Eddard recants the claims he has made about Joffrey not being the true king. \\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/1a/Ned%27s_execution.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160730054118" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Ned&amp;#039;s execution"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Ned%27s_execution.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Ned&#39;s execution.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/1a/Ned%27s_execution.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160730054118"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="101"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/1a/Ned%27s_execution.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160730054118" \\t alt="Ned&amp;#039;s execution"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Ned%27s_execution.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Ned&#39;s execution.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="101"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Ned%27s_execution.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei, Joffrey, and Sansa watch as Ned is executed.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Sansa is sure he will.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">[15]</a></sup> Cersei is present at the Sept of Baelor when Eddard Stark \\\'confesses\\\' his crimes, in accordance with the arrangement brokered by Sansa and <a href="/wiki/Varys" title="Varys">Varys</a>. She is visibly horrified when Joffrey arrogantly flouts the arrangement and instead demands Eddard\\\'s decapitation. Knowing that this will only lead to another war, she frantically tries to persuade her son to reconsider, but the order is nonetheless carried out by Ser <a href="/wiki/Ilyn_Payne" title="Ilyn Payne">Ilyn Payne</a>, the royal executioner.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">[16]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/05/Cersei_and_Lancel.png/revision/latest?cb=20110622114212" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Cersei and Lancel"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cersei_and_Lancel.png" \\tdata-image-name="Cersei and Lancel.png" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/05/Cersei_and_Lancel.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110622114212"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="112"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/05/Cersei_and_Lancel.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110622114212" \\t alt="Cersei and Lancel"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cersei_and_Lancel.png" \\tdata-image-name="Cersei and Lancel.png" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="112"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Cersei_and_Lancel.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei orders Lancel into bed.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Sure enough, war erupts between the Lannister and Stark armies in the <a href="/wiki/Riverlands" title="Riverlands" class="mw-redirect">Riverlands</a> and Cersei attempts to secure her son\\\'s hold on the Iron Throne. She takes a new lover, her cousin <a href="/wiki/Lancel_Lannister" title="Lancel Lannister">Lancel</a> who was King Robert\\\'s squire and gave him the wine that made him too drunk to slay the boar that killed him. She also receives a letter informing her of Jaime\\\'s capture by Robb Stark.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">[17]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Season_2"><a href="/wiki/Season_2" title="Season 2">Season 2</a></span></h3>\\n<p>Cersei continues to govern from <a href="/wiki/King%27s_Landing" title="King\\\'s Landing">King\\\'s Landing</a> as the Queen Regent to <a href="/wiki/Joffrey_Baratheon" title="Joffrey Baratheon">Joffrey</a>. She is driven to defend Joffrey\\\'s claim in the face of several challengers in the <a href="/wiki/War_of_the_Five_Kings" title="War of the Five Kings">War of the Five Kings</a>. Facing imminent winter, she orders the city gates barred to prevent further refugees from entering the city. She is perturbed by the arrival of her brother <a href="/wiki/Tyrion_Lannister" title="Tyrion Lannister">Tyrion</a>, who has been named acting <a href="/wiki/Hand_of_the_King" title="Hand of the King">Hand of the King</a> by their father <a href="/wiki/Tywin_Lannister" title="Tywin Lannister">Tywin Lannister</a>. She fears that Tyrion schemes to usurp her power and is frustrated when he tells her that since she failed to prevent the death of <a href="/wiki/Eddard_Stark" title="Eddard Stark">Eddard Stark</a>, she has been viewed as the disappointing child by Tywin. Tyrion wins her temporary acceptance when he pledges to free <a href="/wiki/Jaime_Lannister" title="Jaime Lannister">Jaime</a> from captivity, but insists that they need to find the fugitive <a href="/wiki/Arya_Stark" title="Arya Stark">Arya Stark</a> in order to facilitate a prisoner exchange.<sup id="cite_ref-E11_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E11-17">[18]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a Arya Stark.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p><a href="/wiki/Stannis_Baratheon" title="Stannis Baratheon">Stannis Baratheon</a> sends copies of a letter detailing Cersei\\\'s incestuous relationship with Jaime and the illegitimacy of her children to high lords throughout the seven kingdoms, fueling widespread rumors. Cersei tasks <a href="/wiki/Petyr_Baelish" title="Petyr Baelish">Petyr Baelish</a> with recovering Arya and is enraged when Baelish dares to reference the rumors. She asks Joffrey to enlist the aid of Tywin in the search, but he refuses to involve his grandfather. He provokes an argument with Cersei about the rumors and threatens her life when she slaps him. He then orders a citywide massacre of <a href="/wiki/Robert_Baratheon" title="Robert Baratheon">Robert Baratheon</a>\\\'s bastard children so that he will have no rival claimants in case his true parentage is revealed.<sup id="cite_ref-E11_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E11-17">[18]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Cersei rejects King <a href="/wiki/Robb_Stark" title="Robb Stark">Robb Stark</a>\\\'s peace terms and refuses a request for aid from the <a href="/wiki/Night%27s_Watch" <a href="/wiki/Jeor_Mormont" title="Jeor Mormont">Mormont</a>. Tyrion ousts Lord <a href="/wiki/Janos_Slynt" title="Janos Slynt">Janos Slynt</a> as commander of the <a href="/wiki/City_Watch" title="City Watch" class="mw-redirect">City Watch</a> for his part in the massacre as well as his betrayal of Ned Stark. Cersei angrily confronts him for displacing her loyal servant.\\n</p><p>He warns her to consider the importance of the support of her subjects; she is dismissive of his concerns but becomes upset at the weight of responsibility she has born. Tyrion mocks her relationship with Jaime. She ends the discussion by saying that Tyrion\\\'s finest joke was killing their mother when he was born.<sup id="cite_ref-The_Night_Lands_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-The_Night_Lands-2">[3]</a></sup>\\n</p><p>Tyrion tests the loyalty of the remaining <a href="/wiki/Small_council" title="Small council">small council</a> members by feeding each of them a different marriage plan for <a href="/wiki/Myrcella_Baratheon" title="Myrcella Baratheon">Myrcella</a>. Pycelle dutifully informs Cersei of Tyrion\\\'s plans to marry Myrcella into <a href="/wiki/House_Martell" title="House Martell">House Martell</a> of <a href="/wiki/Dorne" title="Dorne">Dorne</a> despite his promise to keep them secret. Cersei confronts Tyrion who insists that the alliance is necessary and that Myrcella will be safer in Dorne. He then has Pycelle arrested for breaking his confidence. Tyrion sends <a href="/wiki/Petyr_Baelish" title="Petyr Baelish">Petyr Baelish</a> to negotiate with <a href="/wiki/Catelyn_Stark" title="Catelyn Stark">Catelyn Stark</a>, leaving <a href="/wiki/Varys" title="Varys">Varys</a> as the last active member of Cersei\\\'s small council in the city.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">[19]</a></sup>\\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Robb_Stark" title="Robb Stark">Robb Stark</a> wins a major victory at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Oxcross" title="Battle of Oxcross">Battle of Oxcross</a>. Joffrey responds by having <a href="/wiki/Sansa_Stark" title="Sansa Stark">Sansa Stark</a> publicly beaten, sparing her only because of Cersei\\\'s orders, that if Sansa is killed the Starks will exact vengeance on his uncle Jaime. Tyrion intervenes and halts the ordeal, causing further deterioration in his relationship with Joffrey.<sup id="cite_ref-E14_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E14-19">[20]</a></sup>\\n</p><p>Cersei issues a warrant demanding the release of Pycelle. She tasks her lover and cousin <a href="/wiki/Lancel_Lannister" title="Lancel Lannister">Lancel Lannister</a> with delivering it to Tyrion. Lancel arrives in the middle of the night, and Tyrion asks why he waited so long to deliver the message. When Lancel says he just came from Cersei, Tyrion notices Lancel smells of Cersei\\\'s favorite perfume, and threatens to expose their relationship to Joffrey unless Lancel agrees to become his double agent, reporting everything Cersei does.<sup id="cite_ref-E14_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E14-19">[20]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" class="caption">Cersei keeps her secrets from her brother.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Cersei is pleased when she learns of King <a href="/wiki/Renly_Baratheon" title="Renly Baratheon">Renly Baratheon</a>\\\'s death. Tyrion considers it a sign of an imminent attack by his brother King <a href="/wiki/Stannis_Baratheon" title="Stannis Baratheon">Stannis Baratheon</a>, who has assumed control of Renly\\\'s army. Cersei refuses to discuss measures for the defense of the city and remains irate about the marriage pact with Dorne. Tyrion learns from Lancel that Cersei is relying on the <a href="/wiki/Alchemists%27_Guild" title="Alchemists\\\' Guild">Alchemists\\\' Guild</a> to supply <a href="/wiki/Wildfire" title="Wildfire">Wildfire</a> to defend the city and supplants her relationship with the Guild.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">[21]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/75/206_TOGATN.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170526150156" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="206 TOGATN"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="206_TOGATN.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="206 TOGATN.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/75/206_TOGATN.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170526150156"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="101"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/75/206_TOGATN.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170526150156" \\t alt="206 TOGATN"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="206_TOGATN.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="206 TOGATN.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="101"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:206_TOGATN.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei watches as Myrcella leaves for Dorne.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Cersei and the court assemble at the shore of the <a href="/wiki/Blackwater_Bay" title="Blackwater Bay">Blackwater Bay</a> for the departure of Princess Myrcella. Cersei remains livid about Tyrion\\\'s arrangements for her daughter. She threatens to one day deprive him of someone he loves. As they move through the city to return to the <a href="/wiki/Red_Keep" title="Red Keep">Red Keep</a> they are confronted by angry crowds of starving smallfolk. Joffrey is hit by thrown excrement and triggers a <a href="/wiki/Riot_of_King%27s_Landing" title="Riot of King\\\'s Landing">riot</a> by demanding that his guards kill everyone in the crowd. Tyrion marshals the Lannister guards to lead them to safety.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">[22]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/38/Sansa_and_Cersei.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160814020641" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Sansa and Cersei"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Sansa_and_Cersei.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Sansa and Cersei.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/38/Sansa_and_Cersei.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160814020641"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="104"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/38/Sansa_and_Cersei.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160814020641" \\t alt="Sansa and Cersei"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Sansa_and_Cersei.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Sansa and Cersei.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="104"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Sansa_and_Cersei.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei and Sansa discuss womanhood.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Upon learning that Sansa has <a href="/wiki/Flowering" title="Flowering">flowered</a> for the first time, Cersei summons Sansa and offers her advice on motherhood. Cersei tells her to love only her children, since love makes you weak, although it is a mother\\\'s obligation to love her children. Sansa asks if she should love Joffrey; Cersei replies that she is welcome to try.<sup id="cite_ref-E17_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E17-4">[5]</a></sup>\\n</p><p>Cersei meets with Tyrion to discuss the imminent attack of King\\\'s Landing by King <a href="/wiki/Stannis_Baratheon" title="Stannis Baratheon">Stannis Baratheon</a>. She admits her struggles controlling Joffrey and openly references her relationship with Jaime. She confides her fear that Joffrey\\\'s madness is the price for her sins, including her incestuous relationship. Tyrion tries to comfort her by telling her that Tommen and Myrcella are good, decent children.<sup id="cite_ref-E17_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E17-4">[5]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/38/Lamprey_Pie_2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130818170958" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Lamprey Pie 2"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Lamprey_Pie_2.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Lamprey Pie 2.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/38/Lamprey_Pie_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130818170958"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="101"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/38/Lamprey_Pie_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130818170958" \\t alt="Lamprey Pie 2"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Lamprey_Pie_2.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Lamprey Pie 2.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="101"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Lamprey_Pie_2.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei tells Tyrion of her suspicions.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Joffrey is keen to fight in defense of the city. Cersei is furious and suspects Tyrion of trying to kill her son. She mistakenly identifies <a href="/wiki/Ros" title="Ros">Ros</a> as his lover because of the Lannister necklace Tyrion gave her and seizes the opportunity to deliver on the threat she made when Myrcella left. Cersei has the prostitute kidnapped as insurance against Tyrion placing Joffrey in harms way. She reveals her ploy over dinner and Tyrion vows to free Ros and take revenge when Cersei least suspects it.<sup id="cite_ref-E18_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E18-6">[7]</a></sup>\\n</p><p>Cersei provides refuge for the women of the court in <a href="/wiki/Maegor%27s_Holdfast" title="Maegor\\\'s Holdfast">Maegor\\\'s Holdfast</a> during the battle. She prepares for the worst by having Ser <a href="/wiki/Ilyn_Payne" title="Ilyn Payne">Ilyn Payne</a> present and obtaining deadly <a href="/wiki/Essence_of_Nightshade" title="Essence of Nightshade">Essence of Nightshade</a> poison from the reinstated Pycelle. She drinks heavily during the siege and torments Sansa Stark when she tries to keep up the morale of the women by praying. She tells Sansa that the gods have no mercy and that Ser Ilyn is there to kill them should the Red Keep be breached.\\n</p><p>Lancel is wounded and returns from the walls to report that Stannis has reached the <a href="/wiki/Mud_Gate" title="Mud Gate">Mud Gate</a>, despite Tyrion\\\'s ingenious use of Wildfire to destroy a large portion of his fleet. Cersei sends Lancel to bring Joffrey back to the Red Keep, ignoring his protests that it will damage morale. Joffrey willingly leaves the field but his exit is a blow to the men. \\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/5c/Cersei_and_Tommen_Blackwater_Promo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120529033552" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Cersei and Tommen Blackwater Promo"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cersei_and_Tommen_Blackwater_Promo.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Cersei and Tommen Blackwater Promo.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/5c/Cersei_and_Tommen_Blackwater_Promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120529033552"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="271"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/5c/Cersei_and_Tommen_Blackwater_Promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120529033552" \\t alt="Cersei and Tommen Blackwater Promo"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cersei_and_Tommen_Blackwater_Promo.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Cersei and Tommen Blackwater Promo.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="271"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Cersei_and_Tommen_Blackwater_Promo.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei and Tommen upon Tywin\\\'s return to King\\\'s Landing.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Lancel begs Cersei to let him return Joffrey to the front, believing the battle is lost otherwise. Cersei pushes him into a stone pillar, aggravating his injury, and storms out. Convinced the battle is lost, and not wanting her children to die by Stannis\\\'s hand, she takes Tommen to the Iron Throne room and prepares to poison him. She is stopped just in time by the unexpected arrival of Tywin, who reports that they have won the battle. Tyrion is betrayed and wounded by Ser <a href="/wiki/Mandon_Moore" title="Mandon Moore">Mandon Moore</a> of the Kingsguard during the fighting.<sup id="cite_ref-S2EP09_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S2EP09-22">[23]</a></sup> Tyrion\\\'s role in defending the city is not acknowledged and he is left to recover from his wounds, stripped of his power. Rumors circulate that Cersei ordered the attack on Tyrion. No longer considering Tyrion a threat, Cersei releases Ros.<sup id="cite_ref-E20_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E20-23">[24]</a></sup>\\n</p><p>Cersei orchestrates a public ceremony rewarding those who aided the city in the battle. Tywin is officially recognized as Hand of the King, Petyr Baelish is named Lord of Harrenhal for brokering the alliance with House Tyrell and Ser Loras is offered a favor of his choosing. He asks Joffrey to marry his sister, <a href="/wiki/Margaery_Tyrell" title="Margaery Tyrell">Margaery Tyrell</a>. Joffrey says that he is constrained by his betrothal to Sansa but Cersei intervenes to insist that the treachery of <a href="/wiki/House_Stark" title="House Stark">House Stark</a> frees him from any obligation. The court welcome the decision with a round of applause.<sup id="cite_ref-E20_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E20-23">[24]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Season_3"><a href="/wiki/Season_3" title="Season 3">Season 3</a></span></h3>\\n<p>Some weeks after the Battle of Blackwater,Cersei pays Tyrion a visit accompanied by two of her son\\\'s Kingsguard. She only gains entrance to Tyrion\\\'s chambers after agreeing to leave her guards outside. Once inside Cersei demands to know how he will "slander" her to their father now that he is here. Tyrion asks when he has ever slandered her before, and she reminds him of a time at Casterly Rock that he got her in serious trouble with their father: when she was nine years old, Cersei discovered that a servant girl (also nine years old) had stolen a necklace, so she had her guards beat the girl, who ended up losing an eye. Tyrion told their father what Cersei had done and he was angered, but Cersei notes that the servant girl never stole a necklace again. Tyrion quips that it isn\\\'t "slander" if it\\\'s true, and he only told Tywin what she really did. The queen admits that Tyrion is a clever man but not as clever as he might believe. Tyrion merely retorts that this still makes him a great deal more clever that her. Cersei then leaves abruptly and just in time to prevent Meryn Trant and Bronn from exchanging blows.\\n</p><p>At night, Cersei and Joffrey are hosting a private dinner party for Loras and Margaery Tyrell. Cersei is surprised that Margaery has been handing out food aid to the <a href="/wiki/Smallfolk" title="Smallfolk">smallfolk</a> of the city and visiting orphanages. Unlike Cersei, who only knows how to rule through fear, Margaery is skilled at winning the hearts and minds of the common people, and this concerns Cersei. After trading veiled insults with both her son and future daughter-in-law, it becomes clear that Cersei doesn\\\'t trust Margaery and fears that the younger woman has come to usurp her as queen.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">[25]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a about his upcoming wedding, Cersei begins to criticize Margaery, saying that she is only charitable to the poor to build up her own reputation and that she dresses like a harlot for a reason. Joffrey, however, dismissively tells Cersei off. <sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">[26]</a></sup>\\n</p><p> AtKing\\\'s Landing,Tywin Lannistercalls the first meeting of theSmall Councilsince he arrived in the city and assumed his position asHand of the King. He has the meeting place changed to a room next to his own quarters in theTower of the Hand, asserting his dominance. Tywin arrives early and has all of the council members called in at once. All of the seats are on one side of the table, as a non-verbal test to see how each of them reacts around him.Cerseiarrives tofind the seats are all occupied, but not wanting to play that game and be relegated to a lowly position, she pulls up a chair so she is sitting at Tywin\\\'s right hand, opposite Littlefinger.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">[27]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/a/af/BaelorSeptInside.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160823014932" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img
