\\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>While Joffrey is giving Margaery a tour of the Sept of Baelor, Cersei speaks with Lady <a href="/wiki/Olenna_Tyrell" title="Olenna Tyrell">Olenna</a>, exchanging stories about their deceased husbands. When Margaery takes Joffrey with her to greet the common people, Cersei realizes that she has lost control of Joffrey to the Tyrells. Later, Cersei meets with Tywin to discuss the Tyrells and informs him how Margaery has begun to manipulate Joffrey. Tywin is satisfied, as Cersei has only let Joffrey do whatever he pleased. He also tells her that she is not as smart as she thinks she is and that undermining the Tyrells would be irrational considering how they helped defeat Stannis. When Margaery and Joffrey wave to the crowd outside the Sept, Cersei initially fears for Joffrey\\\'s safety. Upon realizing that the crowd is hailing the two, Cersei then realizes that Margaery has a control over Joffrey.<sup id="cite_ref-E24_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E24-27">[28]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/17/Cersei_Baelish_Kissed_by_Fire.png/revision/latest?cb=20130429060917" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Cersei Baelish Kissed by Fire"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cersei_Baelish_Kissed_by_Fire.png" \\tdata-image-name="Cersei Baelish Kissed by Fire.png" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/17/Cersei_Baelish_Kissed_by_Fire.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130429060917"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="85"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/17/Cersei_Baelish_Kissed_by_Fire.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130429060917" \\t alt="Cersei Baelish Kissed by Fire"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cersei_Baelish_Kissed_by_Fire.png" \\tdata-image-name="Cersei Baelish Kissed by Fire.png" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="85"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Cersei_Baelish_Kissed_by_Fire.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei and Littlefinger</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Cersei encounters Lord Baelish and informs him that she fears the Tyrells do not have the Lannisters\\\' best interest at heart. Littlefinger agrees that he will use his spies to uncover their plans, one of which turns out to be marrying Loras to Sansa. Initially, Cersei is delighted when her father decides to "kill this union in its crib" by instead having Tyrion marry Sansa to secure the North. However, her smug attitude towards Tyrion when this is revealed to him quickly evaporates when Tywin reveals that he intends to have her marry Loras to secure the Reach.\\n</p><p>Cersei protests against this, saying she is Queen Regent and not some broodmare, but Tywin angrily asserts that she is his daughter and she will do what he tells her and put an end to the "rumors" about her. Cersei begs her father not to make her enter another loveless marriage but Tywin refuses to hear another word from either of his children, saying they have disgraced the family name for far too long. As Tywin leaves the room, Cersei hesitantly opens her eyes and shifts her gaze toward Tyrion, expecting to see him laughing at her but Tyrion is too glum about his own awkward predicament.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">[29]</a></sup>\\n</p><p>CerseiandTyrion Lannisterobserve Loras and Sansa from Cersei\\\'s chambers overlooking the garden. Tyrion sarcastically asks which of the four of them has it the worst. He then finally accuses his sister of trying to have him killed during theBattle of the Blackwater. Cersei, tired of fighting him, remains quiet while he deduces that only two people can command the Kingsguard.Tyrionrealizes thatwhile Cersei certainly has the authority to command a Kingsguard, she isn\\\'t stupid enough to command Ser<a href="/wiki/Mandon_Moore" title="Mandon Moore">Mandon Moore</a>to kill him in public. Tyrion realizes that it was in factJoffreywho ordered Ser Mandon Moore to kill him, because Tyrionwas the only one who stood up to him. Cersei tells him his life is not in danger from Joffrey, as he dare not try anything like that now that Tywin is theHand. They discuss about Jaime\\\'s possible return to King\\\'s Landing, with Cersei wondering where he could possibly be. She asks Tyrion which one of them should be the one to break the news to Sansa. Tyrion decides he might as well dash Sansa\\\'s hopes sooner rather than later.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">[30]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/36/Margaery_and_Cersei_Second_Sons.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130530160122" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Margaery and Cersei Second Sons"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Margaery_and_Cersei_Second_Sons.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Margaery and Cersei Second Sons.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/36/Margaery_and_Cersei_Second_Sons.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130530160122"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/36/Margaery_and_Cersei_Second_Sons.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130530160122" \\t alt="Margaery and Cersei Second Sons"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Margaery_and_Cersei_Second_Sons.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Margaery and Cersei Second Sons.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Margaery_and_Cersei_Second_Sons.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei threatens to have <a href="/wiki/Margaery_Tyrell" title="Margaery Tyrell">Margaery Tyrell</a> strangled in her sleep.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>As the court gathers for Tyrion\\\'s wedding, Cersei finally snaps when Margaery says she looks radiant. Cersei reminds the queen-in-waiting of the lyrics of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Rains_of_Castamere_(song)" title="The Rains of Castamere (song)">The Rains of Castamere</a></i> and to take a lesson of what happened to House Reyne. Cersei threatens to have Margaery strangled in her sleep if she ever refers to her as "sister" again. Cersei maintains a cool expression during the ceremony, and does not laugh when Joffrey ridicules Tyrion by removing his footstool. During the wedding feast, Joffrey heads off to torment Sansa some more. Fed up with him, Cersei tells him to speak with Margaery instead, but he ignores her. Cersei later retreats to an upper gallery and stares despondently out over <a href="/wiki/Blackwater_Bay" title="Blackwater Bay">Blackwater Bay</a>. Loras sees her and tries to make small talk, but Cersei rudely brushes him off.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">[31]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/36/Tywin_Joff_and_Cersei_Mhysa.png/revision/latest?cb=20130610045027" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Tywin Joff and Cersei Mhysa"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Tywin_Joff_and_Cersei_Mhysa.png" \\tdata-image-name="Tywin Joff and Cersei Mhysa.png" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/36/Tywin_Joff_and_Cersei_Mhysa.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130610045027"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="109"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/36/Tywin_Joff_and_Cersei_Mhysa.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130610045027" \\t alt="Tywin Joff and Cersei Mhysa"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Tywin_Joff_and_Cersei_Mhysa.png" \\tdata-image-name="Tywin Joff and Cersei Mhysa.png" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="109"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Tywin_Joff_and_Cersei_Mhysa.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei, Tywin and Joffrey listen to Tyrion\\\'s threats.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Cersei is present at the meeting where Tyrion learns of <a href="/wiki/Red_wedding" title="Red wedding" class="mw-redirect">Robb and Catelyn\\\'s deaths</a>. Joffrey comments that he wants to present Robb\\\'s head to Sansa at his wedding feast as promised, though Varys reminds him that Sansa is now his aunt-by-marriage. Cerseibrushes it off as a joke, though Joffreydenies this. She also reassures Joffrey when he is threatened by Tyrion. At the end of the meeting, she leads Joffreyto bed after he calls out Tywin\\\'s cowardice during the <a href="/wiki/Robert%27s_Rebellion" title="Robert\\\'s Rebellion">Rebellion</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-E29_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E29-31">[32]</a></sup>\\n</p><p>Later, Cerseivisits Tyrion and rudely dismisses Podrick. She tellsTyrionthat he should giveSansa a son if he truly wants to make her happy, though Tyrionresponds by asking her if she is happy as she has children. Cersei admits that she is not happy, but would\\\'ve thrown herself "from the highest window in the <a href="/wiki/Red_Keep" title="Red Keep">Red Keep</a>" without them, even Joffrey. She recounts of how he was all she had before Myrcella was born and how she would spend hours looking at him, and acknowledges that he is one of the "terrible ones". Tyrion asks her when <a href="/wiki/War_of_the_Five_Kings" title="War of the Five Kings">this</a> will end, and Cersei replies when they have dealt with all their enemies. Tyrion mentions how dealing with one enemy creates two more, and she just says that they will be in this position for a long time.<sup id="cite_ref-E29_31-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E29-31">[32]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/21/Mhysa_Cersei_finale_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130601164644" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Mhysa Cersei finale image"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Mhysa_Cersei_finale_image.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Mhysa Cersei finale image.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/21/Mhysa_Cersei_finale_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130601164644"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="101"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/21/Mhysa_Cersei_finale_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130601164644" \\t alt="Mhysa Cersei finale image"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Mhysa_Cersei_finale_image.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Mhysa Cersei finale image.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="101"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Mhysa_Cersei_finale_image.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei is reunited with Jaime.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>WhenJaime returns to King\\\'s Landing, he immediately goes to Cersei\\\'s chambers and calls her name. Looking at seashells on her bed, smiling, she turns around upon hearing her name called, shocked and sickened at finding him maimed.<sup id="cite_ref-E29_31-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E29-31">[32]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Season_4"><a href="/wiki/Season_4" title="Season 4">Season 4</a></span></h3>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c0/Got_S4_jaime_and_cersei.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160712035248" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Got S4 jaime and cersei"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Got_S4_jaime_and_cersei.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Got S4 jaime and cersei.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c0/Got_S4_jaime_and_cersei.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160712035248"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c0/Got_S4_jaime_and_cersei.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160712035248" \\t alt="Got S4 jaime and cersei"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Got_S4_jaime_and_cersei.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Got S4 jaime and cersei.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Got_S4_jaime_and_cersei.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei rejects Jaime.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Cersei is present while <a href="/wiki/Qyburn" title="Qyburn">Qyburn</a> is attachingJaime\\\'s golden prosthetic hand that she commissioned for him because she\\\'s so disgusted by his stump. After Qyburn departs from Cersei\\\'schambers, <a href="/wiki/Jaime_Lannister" title="Jaime Lannister">Jaime</a> asks why she drinks more than she used to. Cersei replies that she drinks more because Jaime left the capital, <a href="/wiki/Robert_Baratheon" title="Robert Baratheon">Robert</a> was killed, <a href="/wiki/Myrcella_Baratheon" title="Myrcella Baratheon">Myrcella</a> was shipped off to Dorne, they suffered through a siege, and her son <a href="/wiki/Joffrey_Baratheon" title="Joffrey Baratheon">Joffrey</a> is being married to <a href="/wiki/Margaery_Tyrell" title="Margaery Tyrell">Margaery</a> whom she despises. When Jaime tries to make love to her, she refuses him and says that everythinghas changed and that he took too long to return.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">[33]</a></sup>\\n</p><p>Cerseiis present at the breakfast of Joffrey and Margaery and tells <a href="/wiki/Tywin_Lannister" title="Tywin Lannister">Tywin</a>about <a href="/wiki/Shae" title="Shae">Shae</a> being seen leaving Tyrion\\\'s chambers. During the <a href="/wiki/Purple_Wedding" title="Purple Wedding">wedding feast</a>, Cerseisits with the rest of the royal family. When <a href="/wiki/Brienne_of_Tarth" title="Brienne of Tarth">Brienne of Tarth</a>approaches the king and Margaery, she bows and congratulates them on their marriage. \\n</p><p>Cerseiquickly points out that she bowed instead of performing a curtsy. She then thanks Briennefor bringing her brother back and asks her if she loves Jaime. Brienne responds by walking off.<sup id="cite_ref-E32_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E32-33">[34]</a></sup>\\n</p><p>After Margaery says that the leftovers are going to the poor, Cersei kisses her on the cheek and says she is an inspiration to them all. Shortly after, she goes over to <a href="/wiki/Pycelle" title="Pycelle">Pycelle</a>, who is harassing a young woman. Cersei tells Pycelle to leave her alone and says that she should get Qyburnto examine her. Pycellemocks Qyburn, but Cersei responds by ordering Pycelleto go to the kitchens and order the cooks to give the leftovers to the dogs instead. Pycelle is reluctant to do so, but Cerseithreatens to have him killed if he does not. Cersei and Tywin meet <a href="/wiki/Oberyn_Martell" title="Oberyn Martell">Oberyn</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ellaria_Sand" title="Ellaria Sand">Ellaria</a> and the four get into a heated discussion when Cersei hypocritically mocks Ellaria\\\'s baseborn origins despite the fact that her own children are also bastards (and born out of incest no less). \\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c0/Joffrey_points.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140414190812" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Joffrey points"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Joffrey_points.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Joffrey points.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c0/Joffrey_points.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140414190812"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="101"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c0/Joffrey_points.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140414190812" \\t alt="Joffrey points"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Joffrey_points.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Joffrey points.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="101"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Joffrey_points.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei holds Joffrey as he dies.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Joffrey then makes his speech, publicly embarrassing Tyrion, much to Cersei\\\'s delight. Joffrey then begins to choke on his wine, causing him to gasp for air and collapse. Cersei rushes over to her son, who points towards Tyrion. He then dies in her arms, blood flowing from his eyes and mouth from the effects of the<a href="/wiki/The_strangler" title="The strangler"> strangler</a>. In a blind rage, she accuses <a href="/wiki/Tyrion_Lannister" title="Tyrion Lannister">Tyrion</a> and has him arrested. Upon noticing that Sansa has vanished, she immediately begins to suspect her too and petulantly demands to know her whereabouts.<sup id="cite_ref-E32_33-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E32-33">[34]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/3e/Jaime_and_Cersei_-_Breaker_of_Chains.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160716033631" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Jaime and Cersei - Breaker of Chains"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Jaime_and_Cersei_-_Breaker_of_Chains.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Jaime and Cersei - Breaker of Chains.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/3e/Jaime_and_Cersei_-_Breaker_of_Chains.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160716033631"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="111"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/3e/Jaime_and_Cersei_-_Breaker_of_Chains.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160716033631" \\t alt="Jaime and Cersei - Breaker of Chains"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Jaime_and_Cersei_-_Breaker_of_Chains.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Jaime and Cersei - Breaker of Chains.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="111"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Jaime_and_Cersei_-_Breaker_of_Chains.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Jaime tempts Cersei within the Great Sept of Baelor.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Cersei is mourning Joffrey while Tywin arrives and immediately begins instructing Tommen on the qualities of a good king, much to her annoyance. After the two leave, Jaime arrives to comfort Cersei. She breaks down into tears and asks Jaime to avenge their son by killing Tyrion. Jaime is not convinced that Tyrion was behind the murder and tells Cersei that there will be a trial, but she does not care. He tries to comfort her through his affections. Cersei refuses initially, but Jaime is aggressive. Cersei insists that the sept during a private viewing of their son\\\'s corpse is a highly inappropriate place for sex, and asks Jaime to stop, saying "It isn\\\'t right, it isn\\\'t right..." and Jaime refuses to stop, saying, "I don\\\'t care, I don\\\'t care...". They proceed to embrace and have rough, angry sex on the floor next to Joffrey\\\'s corpse.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">[35]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<dl><dd><i>See main article: "<a href="/wiki/The_Jaime/Cersei_sex_scene_in_%22Breaker_of_Chains%22" title="The Jaime/Cersei sex scene in &quot;Breaker of Chains&quot;" class="mw-redirect">The Jaime/Cersei sex scene in "Breaker of Chains"</a>.</i>\\n</dd></dl>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/37/Jaime_and_Cersei_-_Oathkeeper.png/revision/latest?cb=20140529130606" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Jaime and Cersei - She then asks why Catelyn Stark released him from his captivity. Jaime replies that he swore by all the gods that he would bring back Catelyn Stark\\\'s daughters to her. Cersei questions his loyalty to their enemies, but Jaime states that he only did it so he could return to her. She then asks if he could track down and kill Sansa Stark, believing that she schemed with Tyrion to murder Joffrey. Jaime remains silent. He then tries to convince Cersei that Tyrion is innocent, but she refutes that he has always pitied their little brother and firmly believes that Tyrion is the monster that killed their son. Cersei tells Jaime that she wants four men at Tommen\\\'s door and abruptly dismisses him, referring to him only as "Lord Commander", showing that their relationship has almost completely deteriorated.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">[36]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a Pycelle offers his condolences, yet she completely ignores him as well. She is then approached by Lancel, who has recovered from his wounds at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Blackwater" title="Battle of the Blackwater">Blackwater</a> and become extremely pious and joined the <a href="/wiki/Sparrows" title="Sparrows">Sparrows</a>. <a href="/wiki/Kevan_Lannister" title="Kevan Lannister">Kevan</a> apologizes for the appearance of his son, but Cersei comforts him by saying Lancel will grow out of this phase. While she is having a private moment, Lancel approaches her again and asks for her forgiveness for their "unnatural" relationship, and for serving Robert the wine that led to his death. Cersei brushes off Lancel\\\'s request, and his prayers for Tywin\\\'s soul.<sup id="cite_ref-S5EP01_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S5EP01-5">[6]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0a/Cersei_Season_5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150425040709" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Cersei Season 5"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cersei_Season_5.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Cersei Season 5.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0a/Cersei_Season_5.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150425040709"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0a/Cersei_Season_5.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150425040709" \\t alt="Cersei Season 5"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cersei_Season_5.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Cersei Season 5.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Cersei_Season_5.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei speaks with Jaime about retrieving Myrcella from Dorne.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Cersei summons Jaime to show him a box she\\\'s received. Inside, a stuffed Red Viper holds Myrcella\\\'s necklace in its jaws. Cersei is both unnerved and unsurprised by the threat as Dorne blames the Lannisters for the deaths of Oberyn and Elia Martell. Acknowledging Cersei\\\'s distress, Jaime makes a promise: "I\\\'m going to Dorne. And I\\\'m bringing our daughter home." When Jaime asks Bronn to join him in this quest, he reveals that Cersei has arranged for <a href="/wiki/Willas_Bracken" title="Willas Bracken" class="mw-redirect">Willas Bracken</a> to wed Lollys Stokeworth instead of Bronn, breaking their agreement.\\n</p><p>Later, <a href="/wiki/Dwarf_hunter_1" title="Dwarf hunter 1">two</a> <a href="/wiki/Dwarf_hunter_2" title="Dwarf hunter 2">men</a> bring Cersei the head of a dwarf. She\\\'s disappointed it\\\'s not her brother, but donates the head to Qyburn\\\'s lab. Cersei presides over the <a href="/wiki/Small_Council" title="Small Council" class="mw-redirect">Small Council</a> and doles out new titles on Tommen\\\'s behalf: Qyburn is named Master of Whisperers, and Mace Tyrell takes on the additional title of Master of Coin. When Cersei appoints her uncle Kevan as Master of War, he rejects the offer. "I did not return to the capital to serve as your puppet," he says, emphasizing that Tommen should attend the meetings himself. Kevan reminds Cersei she\\\'s nothing more than Queen Mother, and he decides to return to Casterly Rock. Cersei is left dissatisfied with Kevan\\\'s departure.<sup id="cite_ref-S5EP02_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S5EP02-41">[42]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/7b/Game_of_Throne_Season_5_04.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150131021458" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Game of Throne Season 5 04"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Game_of_Throne_Season_5_04.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Game of Throne Season 5 04.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/7b/Game_of_Throne_Season_5_04.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150131021458"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/7b/Game_of_Throne_Season_5_04.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150131021458" \\t alt="Game of Throne Season 5 04"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Game_of_Throne_Season_5_04.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Game of Throne Season 5 04.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Game_of_Throne_Season_5_04.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Tommen asks Cersei of Casterly Rock.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>On the way to the Sept of Baelor, Cersei is incensed to find the crowd cheering Margaery\\\'s name. She remains stone-faced throughout the ceremony. The following morning, Cersei walks with Tommen along the battlements and tries to subtly turn him against his wife, but Tommen scares her by asking her if she\\\'d prefer to go back to Casterly Rock. Cersei goes to confront Margaery, finding her bragging about Tommen\\\'s libido to her handmaidens. Cersei tries to verbally spar with Margaery as she used to, but the younger queen is in her prime, and assaults Cersei with backhanded compliments and subtle barbs. Realizing that she is losing, Cersei departs. \\nLater on, Cersei and the Small Council are visited by the <a href="/wiki/High_Septon_(After_the_riot_of_King%27s_Landing)" title="High Septon (After the riot of King\\\'s Landing)">High Septon</a>, who has recently been abducted from Littlefinger\\\'s brothel and forced to walk naked through the streets of King\\\'s Landing. Cersei is mildly amused and not particularly sympathetic to the man\\\'s plight. She later pays a visit to the so-called <a href="/wiki/High_Sparrow" title="High Sparrow">High Sparrow</a>. Assuming a much more conciliatory and humble tone than she ever has before, Cersei talks with him about the relationship between the Faith and the Crown, and also mentions that she\\\'s had the High Septon thrown in the <a href="/wiki/Black_Cells" title="Black Cells">Black Cells</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">[43]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/24/Cersei_high_sparrow_Sons_of_the_Harpy.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160809141349" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei greets the High Sparrow.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Cersei meets with the High Sparrow again and names him as the new High Septon, allowing him to reinstate the <a href="/wiki/Faith_Militant" title="Faith Militant">Faith Militant</a>, a military order dedicated to defending the Faith of the Seven which was abolished two centuries ago. Loras Tyrell is arrested during the ensuing rampage for his homosexuality, which Margaery believes is part of Cersei\\\'s plan to divide her and Tommen. \\n</p><p>Tommen confronts his mother and demands that Loras be released, but she calmly tells him that she didn\\\'t order his arrest, although her tone of voice seems to imply that she knew beforehand that Loras would be arrested and allowed it to happen in order to interfere with Margaery and Tommen\\\'s relationship.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">[44]</a></sup>\\n</p><p>During her meetings with Littlefinger, Cersei again feigns ignorance about Loras\\\' arrest and seems unconcerned about what repercussions this might have. The Queen Regent is about to dismiss Baelish when he admits that even though he lost track of Arya, he has discovered Sansa Stark\\\'s whereabouts.  \\nShe\\\'s finally back at Winterfell \\\'allying\\\' herself with House Bolton. Cersei is naturally livid that the Boltons have betrayed her and vows that they\\\'ll end up being flayed for their crimes. Petyr then suggests that Cersei could just wait a while until Stannis has dealt with the Boltons or vice versa. The Vale army (under his command) could later easily mop up the remains. The only boon Littlefinger wants for his service is to be named Warden of the North. Cersei readily agrees on the condition that Baelish brings her Sansa\\\'s head.\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/08/Game-of-thrones-unbowed-unbent-unbroken-tommen-cersei.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160814015353" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t trial.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\nAfter a brief but tense meeting with <a href="/wiki/Olenna_Tyrell" title="Olenna Tyrell">Olenna</a> in which mutual insults are exchanged, Cersei takes part in the trial of Loras Tyrell. Though she appears incredulous towards the accusations, it is clear that she has played a part in engineering the entire process. She plays the same trump card that she once did with Tyrion and Shae by making a deal with <a href="/wiki/Olyvar" title="Olyvar">Olyvar</a>, Loras\\\'s lover, to testify against Loras in exchange for being spared from persecution. As a result of her schemes, Loras is to be put on trial, and Margaery is imprisoned for giving false testimony.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">[45]</a></sup><figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/8/89/The_Gift_04.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150521210757" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="The Gift 04"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="The_Gift_04.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="The Gift 04.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/8/89/The_Gift_04.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150521210757"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/8/89/The_Gift_04.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150521210757" \\t alt="The Gift 04"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="The_Gift_04.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="The Gift 04.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:The_Gift_04.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei tells Tommen of her love for him.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>When Tommen loses his appetite over his wife\\\'s arrest, Cersei attempts to calm him down, and gives him a long speech about how as King, he will be faced with many circumstantial situations in which he will be powerless to act, as Robert Baratheon sometimes was, though she proclaims her love for him by claiming that she will do anything it takes to protect him, even if it means burning down entire cities, and weeps as she cuddles her son. She later visits Margaery in her cell, bringing her food and trying to convince her that she will do her utmost to get her out, but Margaery angrily counters that she knows Cersei engineered both her arrest and Loras\\\'s in order to retain control over her son, and shouts at her to get out, throwing the bowl of stew at her and calling her a "hateful bitch". Cersei leaves and finds the High Sparrow beneath the Sept of Baelor, who tells her that both Loras and Margaery will be put on trial, and certain septons, including himself, will stand as judges. \\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/b/b6/TheGiftUnellaCersei.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160814023331" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="TheGiftUnellaCersei"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="TheGiftUnellaCersei.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="TheGiftUnellaCersei.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/b/b6/TheGiftUnellaCersei.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160814023331"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="115"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/b/b6/TheGiftUnellaCersei.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160814023331" \\t alt="TheGiftUnellaCersei"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="TheGiftUnellaCersei.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="TheGiftUnellaCersei.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="115"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:TheGiftUnellaCersei.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei is arrested by the Faith Militant for her crimes.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Cersei thanks the High Sparrow for his actions, and he proceeds to give her a speech about the history of the Sept. He tells her that the Tyrells\\\' falsehoods will be revealed for all the world to see, as in the case of everyone, including Cersei herself. The High Sparrow reveals that Lancel confessed his adulterous affair with Cersei following Jaime\\\'s capture by Robb Stark, and orders Cersei arrested, to her horror. She is taken to a cell by a group of septas, but threatens them that her face is the last thing they will see before they die for what they are doing to her.<sup id="cite_ref-S05EP07_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S05EP07-45">[46]</a></sup>\\n</p><p>Cersei remains in custody for the next few days, visited only by Septa <a href="/wiki/Unella" title="Unella">Unella</a>, who offers her water in return for a confession, but she repeatedly refuses. She is later visited by Qyburn, who informs her that the charges against her are treason, incest and regicide, which she dismisses as lies, though Qyburn reminds her that the Faith will not depend on physical proof as much as the Crown does in her upcoming trial. She asks about Jaime, but Qyburn claims there has been no response, and further tells her that Pycelle has summoned Kevan back to the capital and Tommen has fallen into a depression.\\n</p><p>Qyburn, however, tells Cersei that she can still confess, but she refuses. Before he leaves, Qyburn tells her that his work is progressing. Later, when Unella visits her again, Cersei offers to make her a Lady of the capital or have her killed, depending on whether or not she will help her. Unella pours her water on the floor and leaves. Cersei finally abandons her pride and licks the water from the dungeon floor, breaking into tears.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">[47]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/f9/Mother%27s_mercy_high_sparrow_cersei.png/revision/latest?cb=20150625200513" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Mother&amp;#039;s mercy high sparrow cersei"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Mother%27s_mercy_high_sparrow_cersei.png" \\tdata-image-name="Mother&#39;s mercy high sparrow cersei.png" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/f9/Mother%27s_mercy_high_sparrow_cersei.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150625200513"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="101"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/f9/Mother%27s_mercy_high_sparrow_cersei.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150625200513" \\t alt="Mother&amp;#039;s mercy high sparrow cersei"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Mother%27s_mercy_high_sparrow_cersei.png" \\tdata-image-name="Mother&#39;s mercy high sparrow cersei.png" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="101"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Mother%27s_mercy_high_sparrow_cersei.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei pleads for freedom.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Sometime later, Cersei is brought before the High Sparrow to confess her sins. She confesses of adultery with Ser Lancel Lannister, but denies her incestuous relationship with her brother Jaime. She begs to be allowed to go to the Red Keep to see her son Tommen. The High Sparrow accepts, but states that she has to stand trial. \\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/60/WalkOfAtonement.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20190409221315" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="WalkOfAtonement"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="WalkOfAtonement.jpeg" \\tdata-image-name="WalkOfAtonement.jpeg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/60/WalkOfAtonement.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190409221315"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="101"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/60/WalkOfAtonement.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190409221315" \\t alt="WalkOfAtonement"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="WalkOfAtonement.jpeg" \\tdata-image-name="WalkOfAtonement.jpeg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="101"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:WalkOfAtonement.jpeg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei endures her walk of atonement.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Cersei is brought to a cell where she is stripped naked and washed before her hair is cut short. She is brought outside were she has to walk naked through the streets of Kings Landing from the Great Sept of Baelor to the Red Keep as punishment. She is escorted through an angry mob who hurl filth and vicious insults at her.\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/e2/Mountainstein.png/revision/latest?cb=20150926114135" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Mountainstein"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Mountainstein.png" \\tdata-image-name="Mountainstein.png" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/e2/Mountainstein.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150926114135"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="101"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/e2/Mountainstein.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150926114135" \\t alt="Mountainstein"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Mountainstein.png" \\tdata-image-name="Mountainstein.png" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="101"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Mountainstein.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei, with vengeance in her eyes, is carried by the Mountain.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>With bloody feet Cersei makes it to the Red Keep. Upon entering the gates, Cersei finds her uncle <a href="/wiki/Kevan_Lannister" title="Kevan Lannister">Kevan Lannister</a>, Grand Maester Pycelle and Qyburn waiting for her. Qyburn attempts to comfort her by covering her body with a cloak. Heavy footsteps are heard, and Qyburn introduces Cersei to the newest member of the Kingsguard: a seven foot tall man in golden armor, the Mountain, who has his face hidden constantly due to Qyburn\\\'s experimentation and the effects of <a href="/wiki/Manticores" title="Manticores">manticore</a> venom. Qyburn suggests Cersei to go inside to have a look at her feet, which are badly injured, when the huge knight lifts her up and carries her away.<sup id="cite_ref-E50_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E50-47">[48]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Season_6"><a href="/wiki/Season_6" title="Season 6">Season 6</a></span></h3>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/a/ac/GOT_S6_03.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160308212058" \\t alt="GOT S6 03"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="GOT_S6_03.png" \\tdata-image-name="GOT S6 03.png" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="101"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:GOT_S6_03.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei is comforted by Jaime following the death of Myrcella.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Once again residing in the Red Keep, Cersei is alerted to Jaime\\\'s return and runs excitedly to the port to meet Myrcella for the first time in the space of almost 4 years, but her worst fears are realized when she sees a despondent Jaime standing alone on the boat, with a corpse behind him she immediately realizes is Myrcella\\\'s. \\nLater, Cersei is comforted by Jaime in her quarters. Cersei finally admits to Jaime that she believes their children\\\'s deaths truly are destined according to Maggy\\\'s prophecy, since both Joffrey and Myrcella are gone and the only one left is Tommen. Jaime scoffs it off and promises Cersei revenge for all that their enemies have taken from them.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">[49]</a></sup>\\n</p><p>A man in King\\\'s Landing brags about revealing himself to Cersei during her walk of shame. When the man leaves the crowd to urinate, the gigantic Kingsguard knight walks up behind him and brutally kills him by smashing his head against the wall before reporting back to Cersei. \\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/ef/Home_25.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160814015014" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Home 25"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Home_25.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Home 25.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/ef/Home_25.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160814015014"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="118"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/ef/Home_25.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160814015014" \\t alt="Home 25"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Home_25.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Home 25.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="118"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Home_25.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei speaks with her son.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>When Cersei attempts to leave for Myrcella\\\'s funeral with the Kingsguard knight in tow, a squad of guards blocks her path; their leader informs her that by order of the King, she is prohibited from leaving the castle, in the interest of her own protection. Cersei demands that they move, but the guards do not budge, even when Cersei\\\'s Kingsguard places a hand on his sword. Eventually, Cersei acquiesces and retreats to her chambers. Tommen later visits his mother to apologize for doing nothing when she was arrested and forced to walk through the streets naked, then asks her to teach him to rule. Moved, Cersei tearfully embraces her son.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">[50]</a></sup>\\n</p><p>Cersei and Jaime later visit Qyburn in his lab, where he has swayed some of Varys\\\'s little birds into his service, to Cersei\\\'s amusement. When Jaime asks Qyburn to order Gregor Clegane to slaughter the High Sparrow and the Faith Militant, Cersei claims it will not be necessary, since she has opted for a trial by combat and again named Gregor as her champion. \\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0e/Oathbreaker_23.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160512164228" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Oathbreaker 23"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Oathbreaker_23.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Oathbreaker 23.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0e/Oathbreaker_23.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160512164228"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0e/Oathbreaker_23.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160512164228" \\t alt="Oathbreaker 23"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Oathbreaker_23.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Oathbreaker 23.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Oathbreaker_23.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei and Jaime intrude on a Small Council meeting.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>She then orders Qyburn to place his spies all over Westeros to prevent any other Great Houses from benefiting from the Lannisters\\\' disgrace. Cersei, Jaime and Gregor attend a Small Council meeting, but Kevan, Pycelle, Olenna and Mace Tyrell refuse to accept them, with Olenna coldly reminding Cersei that she is no longer Queen. When they defy the council and sit down, Kevan leads the council out, leaving Cersei alone with Jaime and Gregor.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">[51]</a></sup>\\n</p><p>A few days later, Cersei goes to speak to Tommen, only to find he is already being counseled by Pycelle. Despite the Grand Maester\\\'s claim that he is simply offering his wisdom to the King, Cersei coldly orders him to leave. Once alone, Cersei wishes to speak with Tommen in private, having missed the past several Small Council meetings. Tommen is anxious to fight the High Sparrow, since Margaery is still a prisoner, though Cersei reminds him of what the Sparrow <a href="/wiki/Walk_of_atonement" title="Walk of atonement">forced her to do</a>. Although Tommen knows his mother has always hated Margaery, Cersei claims the rivalry is unimportant, explaining that kings and queens must command respect, and the High Sparrow is little more than an idealistic anarchist using the Faith to achieve his goals. After Tommen reveals his conversation with the High Sparrow and knowledge of something important, Cersei presses him for information.<sup id="cite_ref-S06E04_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S06E04-51">[52]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/11/Book_of_the_Stranger_14.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160512165557" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Book of the Stranger 14"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Book_of_the_Stranger_14.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Book of the Stranger 14.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/11/Book_of_the_Stranger_14.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160512165557"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/11/Book_of_the_Stranger_14.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160512165557" \\t alt="Book of the Stranger 14"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Book_of_the_Stranger_14.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Book of the Stranger 14.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Book_of_the_Stranger_14.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei tells Kevan and Olenna of her plan.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Cersei and Jaime attend another Small Council meeting, this time presided over by Kevan and Olenna. Though Olenna reminds Cersei she is not welcome, adding her repeated humiliations, Jaime defends his sister, revealing that Tommen has been talking to the High Sparrow about Margaery and Loras. Cersei points out the High Sparrow was expecting them to fight among each other, and before the trial, Margaery will perform her own walk of atonement, which Olenna agrees must not happen. Although Cersei promises to destroy the Sparrows for corrupting Lancel, Kevan warns them the High Sparrow has many supporters, and more lives could be lost in the ensuing battle.<sup removal from the Kingsguard</a>, Jaime informs Cersei he is being sent to Riverrun to help the Freys deal with <a href="/wiki/Brynden_Tully" title="Brynden Tully">Brynden Tully</a>. Despite her brother\\\'s protests and anger over Tommen\\\'s decision to join the High Sparrow, Cersei advises him to lead the Lannister army as their father intended, confident that the Mountain will win her trial by combat. She kisses Jaime goodbye, reminding him they are the only ones who matter.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">[53]</a></sup>  \\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/71/The_Broken_Man_01.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160601190541" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="The Broken Man 01"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="The_Broken_Man_01.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="The Broken Man 01.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/71/The_Broken_Man_01.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160601190541"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/71/The_Broken_Man_01.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160601190541" \\t alt="The Broken Man 01"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="The_Broken_Man_01.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="The Broken Man 01.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:The_Broken_Man_01.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Olenna expresses the futility of the Rise of the Sparrows to Cersei.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Cersei visits Olenna Tyrell in an attempt to convince her to stay in King\\\'s Landing. She uses Margaery and Loras as an excuse for Olenna to stay, but Olenna angrily reminds Cersei that all this is happening because of Cersei herself. Olenna reminds her of the smug look she gave her when Loras and Margaery were being dragged away by the Faith Militant. She tells Cersei that the universally hated Queen Mother has no support in King\\\'s Landing, and has lost.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">[54]</a></sup> \\nQyburn enters Cersei\\\'s chamber to inform her that the Faith Militant have entered the Red Keep. Accompanied by Qyburn and the Mountain, Cersei confronts the group. Lancel tells her that the High Sparrow wishes to speak with her at the Sept of Baelor. When she refuses, Lancel tells her that it is not a request. \\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/a/a4/No_One_01.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160807225710" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="No One 01"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="No_One_01.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="No One 01.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/a/a4/No_One_01.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160807225710"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="117"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/a/a4/No_One_01.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160807225710" \\t alt="No One 01"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="No_One_01.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="No One 01.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="117"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:No_One_01.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei chooses violence.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Cersei retorts that the High Sparrow promised that she could stay in the Red Keep until her trial, which Lancel replies that no such promise was made. When SerGregor Cleganethreatens the Faith Militant, Lancel tells Cersei to order him aside or there would be violence. Cersei says that she chooses violence. One of the Faith Militant attacks the Kingsguard, leaving several visible holes in his armor but drawing no blood. In response, the Mountain rips the man\\\'s head off and tosses it aside and Lancel and his men back down.\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0a/No_One_12.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160807231147" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="No One 12"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="No_One_12.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="No One 12.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0a/No_One_12.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160807231147"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="115"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0a/No_One_12.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160807231147" \\t alt="No One 12"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="No_One_12.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="No One 12.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="115"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:No_One_12.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei is escorted to the Throne Room by Gregor.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Later, Cersei, Qyburn and Ser Gregor enter the Great Hall to find a large crowd gathered for a royal announcement.The ladies in court look at the Queen Mother in detest. Cersei asksKevan Lannisterwhy she was not informed. Kevan bars her from standing beside her son and tells her that her place was in the gallery "with the other ladies of the court". Cersei reluctantly takes her place there while the other women stand aside, not wanting to be near her or Gregor.\\nKing Tommen Baratheonstarts by saying that the Crown andthe Faithare the two pillars that hold up this world, and should one collapse, so does the other. He also says thatThe Fatherjudges them all, and if they break his laws, they shall be punished. He announces thatLoras Tyrelland Cersei\\\'s trial will be held in the Sept of Baelor on the first day of the festival ofThe Mother. After much prayer and reflection, he also announces thattrial by combatwill be forbidden in the Seven Kingdoms, stating that it is a scheme made by those who wants to escape true judgement from the Gods, and that Loras and Cersei would stand trial before seven septonsas it was in the earlier days of the Faith.\\n</p><p>As the King leaves, Qyburn tells a shocked Cersei, who had been planning on calling a trial by combat with Gregor as her champion, that his little birds have been investigating an old rumor that she had told him about, and that it appears to be much more than a rumor.\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a having no intention of going.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>On the day of her trial, Cersei dresses incredibly ornately. She is adorned with fine clothes and all manners of jewelry. However, she does not show up at the Great Sept for her trial, instead viewing the city in the distance from the Red Keep. Unknown to those present at the trial, there is a large cache of wildfire underneath the Sept, placed there by Aerys II at the height of his insanity. Cersei has Qyburn\\\'s little birds light candles with eventually shrink to a size in which the cache can be ignited. Shortly before, Cersei has Qyburn and his little birds murder Pycelle assassinated, so as to consolidate all power to her. \\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/f4/The_Winds_of_Winter_14.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160807082800" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="The Winds of Winter 14"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="The_Winds_of_Winter_14.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="The Winds of Winter 14.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/f4/The_Winds_of_Winter_14.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160807082800"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="118"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/f4/The_Winds_of_Winter_14.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160807082800" \\t alt="The Winds of Winter 14"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="The_Winds_of_Winter_14.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="The Winds of Winter 14.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="118"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:The_Winds_of_Winter_14.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei begins torturing an imprisoned Unella.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\nThe <a href="/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Great_Sept_of_Baelor" title="Destruction of the Great Sept of Baelor">explosion</a> killsMargaery, Mace, and Loras Tyrell, Kevan Lannister, all of the Sparrows including Lancel and the High Sparrow,and a number of King\\\'s Landing citizens. Cersei watches amused and then goes on to "confess her sins" including her incestuous relationship with her brother, the murder of her husband and the explosion of the Great Sept, to capturedSepta Unella. Later she gives her as prisoner to the Mountain, so she can be tortured, calling "Shame" continuously upon her departure. She also states that Unella is not going to die for some time.<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/96/The_Winds_of_Winter_30.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20161215030355" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="The Winds of Winter 30"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="The_Winds_of_Winter_30.jpeg" \\tdata-image-name="The Winds of Winter 30.jpeg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/96/The_Winds_of_Winter_30.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161215030355"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="101"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/96/The_Winds_of_Winter_30.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161215030355" \\t alt="The Winds of Winter 30"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="The_Winds_of_Winter_30.jpeg" \\tdata-image-name="The Winds of Winter 30.jpeg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="101"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:The_Winds_of_Winter_30.jpeg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei becomes the new Queen of the Seven Kingdoms</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Following the <a href="/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Great_Sept_of_Baelor" title="Destruction of the Great Sept of Baelor">destruction of the Sept</a>, Tommen commits suicide by jumping out a window. Cersei orders that his body be burned and the ashes buried at the ruins of the Sept, along with the ashes of her father, elder son and daughter. Through right of conquest, she has Qyburn crown her Queen of the Seven Kingdoms. During the coronation, she sees Jaime from afar, who gives her a grim look.<sup id="cite_ref-S06E10_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S06E10-54">[55]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Season_7"><a href="/wiki/Season_7" title="Season 7">Season 7</a></span></h3>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/2e/GOT_Season_7_18.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170612172757" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="GOT Season 7 18"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="GOT_Season_7_18.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="GOT Season 7 18.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/2e/GOT_Season_7_18.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170612172757"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/2e/GOT_Season_7_18.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170612172757" \\t alt="GOT Season 7 18"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="GOT_Season_7_18.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="GOT Season 7 18.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:GOT_Season_7_18.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei and Jaime discuss Tommen\\\'s death.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Following her coronation, Cersei shows Jaime a giant map of Westeros and discusses the multiple foes they now face. While Cersei has dreams of ushering in a long dynasty, Jaime reminds her that they are losing the war, and with all their children dead, there is no Lannister line to inherit the Iron Throne. When Jaime asks Cersei about Tommen, she responds angrily that he betrayed them by committing suicide. Cersei adds that they are the only living Lannisters who count. Jaime tells her that they need allies and reports that House Frey has been exterminated. Cersei angrily reminds him that she has been listening to their father\\\'s counsel for the past forty years and has learnt some things.\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/5f/GOT_Season_7_22.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170612172800" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="GOT Season 7 22"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="GOT_Season_7_22.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="GOT Season 7 22.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/5f/GOT_Season_7_22.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170612172800"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/5f/GOT_Season_7_22.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170612172800" \\t alt="GOT Season 7 22"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="GOT_Season_7_22.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="GOT Season 7 22.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:GOT_Season_7_22.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei and Jaime meet with Euron Greyjoy.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>They later meet with <a href="/wiki/Euron_Greyjoy" title="Euron Greyjoy">Euron Greyjoy</a> to discuss a possible alliance. Though Cersei declines his offer of marriage, Euron graciously departs, promising to return with a gift that will win her heart.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">[56]</a></sup>Later, Cersei gives a speech urging several nobles from<a href="/wiki/The_Reach" title="The Reach">the Reach</a>, including Lord<a href="/wiki/Randyll_Tarly" title="Randyll Tarly">Randyll Tarly</a>, to reaffirm their allegiance to theIron Throneand not follow House Tyrell in supporting Daenerys. Cersei warns that the Targaryen\\\'s<a href="/wiki/Dothraki" title="Dothraki">Dothraki</a>and<a href="/wiki/Unsullied" title="Unsullied">Unsullied</a>hordes would pillage their lands and homes, and rape their women. When Lord Tarly points out that Daenerys has three dragons,Qyburn replies that he is "at work on a solution".\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/98/Cersei_Qyburn_Machine.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170725182202" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Cersei Qyburn Machine"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cersei_Qyburn_Machine.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Cersei Qyburn Machine.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/98/Cersei_Qyburn_Machine.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170725182202"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/98/Cersei_Qyburn_Machine.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170725182202" \\t alt="Cersei Qyburn Machine"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cersei_Qyburn_Machine.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Cersei Qyburn Machine.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Cersei_Qyburn_Machine.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei and Qyburn test the ballista.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Later, Qyburn leads Cersei to the dragon skulls beneath the Red Keep. He tells Cersei that his spies have reported that one of Daenerys\\\' dragons was wounded by a spear atMeereen, showing that the dragons are not invincible. Qyburn then displays a ballista and reassures her that they can hurt dragons. Cersei tests the ballista on the nearby skull ofBalerionthe Black Dread (the dragon of Aegon the Conqueror) and is pleased when the bolt pierces through the massive, hard skull.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">[57]</a></sup>\\n</p><p>Euron returns to the capital with <a href="/wiki/Ellaria_Sand" title="Ellaria Sand">Ellaria</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tyene_Sand" title="Tyene Sand">Tyene Sand</a>, the women who poisoned her daughter Myrcella. In recognition of Euron\\\'s gesture of good faith, Cersei agrees to Euron\\\'s marriage proposal, though only after the war is won, and names him commander of the Iron Throne\\\'s naval forces. She is cheered by the attendants in the Throne Room following her success, propagandising her defence as being compromised of the "sons and daughters of Westeros".\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/71/Cersei%27s_Prisoners_TQJ.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170731203817" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Cersei&amp;#039;s Prisoners TQJ"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cersei%27s_Prisoners_TQJ.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Cersei&#39;s Prisoners TQJ.jpg" \\t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/71/Cersei%27s_Prisoners_TQJ.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170731203817"  \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  \\t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/71/Cersei%27s_Prisoners_TQJ.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170731203817" \\t alt="Cersei&amp;#039;s Prisoners TQJ"  \\tclass="thumbimage " \\t \\tdata-image-key="Cersei%27s_Prisoners_TQJ.jpg" \\tdata-image-name="Cersei&#39;s Prisoners TQJ.jpg" \\t \\t width="180"  \\t height="120"  \\t \\t \\t \\t></noscript></a>  \\t<figcaption> \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<a href="/wiki/File:Cersei%27s_Prisoners_TQJ.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t \\t\\t\\t<p class="caption">Cersei taunts Ellaria.</p> \\t\\t \\t</figcaption> </figure>\\n<p>Cersei has Ellaria and Tyeneboth chained and gagged in one of the black cells. She tells Ellaria that even though they are enemies, she understands her captive\\\'s fury. She calls to mind how skillful a fighter Oberyn was up to the point when he got killed, taunting Ellaria by insinuating Oberyn brought his own death upon himself by taunting Gregor instead of just leaving him to die. She then reveals her own grief at losing her only daughter, and walks over to Tyene, complimenting her beauty before ungagging her and kissing her full on the lips with the very same <a href="/wiki/Long_farewell" title="Long farewell">poison</a> that Ellaria used on Myrcella. <a href="/wiki/Qyburn" title="Qyburn">Qyburn</a> puts the gag back on Tyene and gives Cersei the antidote.\\n</p><p>Cersei tells Ellaria that she intends to keep her alive to watch Tyene die and rot in the cell, even if they have to force feed her.\\n</p><p>She then expresses her delight by intimately engaging with Jaime, after which she announces that, as Queen, she doesn\\\'t care if servants know of their incest. Then, <a href="/wiki/Bernadette" title="Bernadette">Bernadette</a> arrives, differing from the subject of Jaime, telling Cersei that <a href="/wiki/Tycho_Nestoris" title="Tycho Nestoris">Tycho Nestoris</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Iron_Bank_of_Braavos" title="Iron Bank of Braavos">Iron Bank of Braavos</a> has arrived. Following this she forms an alliance with Tycho, hoping that she will gain a loan after Jaime has successfully taken <a href="/wiki/Highgarden" title="Highgarden">Highgarden</a>. Tycho agrees to this possibility, as Daenerys has cost them many shares in wealth, due to her ending of <a href="/wiki/Slavery" title="Slavery">slavery</a> in <a href="/wiki/Slaver%27s_Bay" title="Slaver\\\'s Bay">Slaver\\\'s Bay</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-E63_57-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E63-57">[58]</a></sup>\\n</p>\\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> \\t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/32/Tycho-Cersei-Spoils-of-War.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170802230700" \\tclass="image image-thumbnail" \\t \\t \\t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \\t alt="Tycho-Cersei-Spoils-of-War"  \\tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \\t
